MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

NOTICE
Resolution of Voluntary Windingup of Company under Section 485(1)
In the matter of the Companies Act, 1956
And
QUICK THREAD PRIVATE LIMITED
(U17231TN1973PTC006353)
Regd. Office: No. 214, Velachery Tambaram Main Road, Pallikkaranai, Chennai-600 100.
At the Extraordinary General Meeting of the members of the company held on 24th day of July 2012, at its registered
office at No. 214, Velachery Tambaram Main Road, Pallikkaranai, Chennai-600 100, the following Special Resolution was
passed unanimously.
RESOLVED THAT pursuant to Section 484(1)(b) and all other applicable provisions of the Companies Act, 1956, the
company be wound up voluntarily.
Chennai,
30th August 2012.

KENNETH VICTOR ABRAHAM,
Liquidator.

MARS CONDUCTORS (INDIA) PRIVATE LIMITED, REGD OFFICE AT 102, NSC BOSE ROAD, CHENNAI-600 079.

Pursuant to Section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956, Notice is hereby given that at an Extraordinary General Meeting
of the Company held on 24th August 2012 the following Special Resolution was passed unanimously to voluntarily wind up
Mars Conductors (India) Private Limited.
RESOLVED THAT having regard to the declaration of solvency dated 23rd July 2012 made by the Board of Directors
of the Company under Section 488 of the Companies Act, 1956, stating that the Company would be able to pay its debts
in full within a period of three years from the date of declaration thereof, the company, having its Registered
Office at 102, NSC Bose Road, 1st Floor, Chennai-600 079, be wound up voluntarily, pursuant to Section 484(1)(b)
of the Companies Act, 1956.
Chennai,
31st August 2012.

For MARS CONDUCTORS (INDIA) PRIVATE LIMITED,
TARUN JAIN,
Director.
